  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0b893196-0437-4df5-8111-87c3a33faae2'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer18101505669432219673">Also available in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded__The_Cosmere_Collection' title='Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection' rel='nofollow noopener'>Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection</a>.<br/><br/>A heretic thief is the empire’s only hope in this fascinating tale that inhabits the same world as the popular novel, <i>Elantris</i>.<br/><br/>Shai is a Forger, a foreigner who can flawlessly copy and re-create any item by rewriting its history with skillful magic. Condemned to death after trying to steal the emperor’s scepter, s</span>
  <span id="freeText18101505669432219673" style="display:none">Also available in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded__The_Cosmere_Collection" title="Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection</a>.<br /><br />A heretic thief is the empire’s only hope in this fascinating tale that inhabits the same world as the popular novel, <i>Elantris</i>.<br /><br />Shai is a Forger, a foreigner who can flawlessly copy and re-create any item by rewriting its history with skillful magic. Condemned to death after trying to steal the emperor’s scepter, she is given one opportunity to save herself. Though her skill as a Forger is considered an abomination by her captors, Shai will attempt to create a new soul for the emperor, who is almost dead. <br /><br />Probing deeply into his life, she discovers Emperor Ashravan’s truest nature—and the opportunity to exploit it. Her only possible ally is one who is truly loyal to the emperor, but councilor Gaotona must overcome his prejudices to understand that Shai’s forgery is as much artistry as it is deception. <br /><br />Brimming with magic and political intrigue, this deftly woven fantasy delves into the essence of a living spirit.</span>

<a href="/questions/6414-why-is-the-emperor-s-soul-considered-to-be">Why is The Emperor&#39;s Soul considered to be set in the universe of Elantris, rather than in the universe of The Way of Kings? Seems to be a much much stronger connection between WOK and TES than Elantris and TES.</a>
</div>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>

<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/3481302-eon-windrunner">Eon ♒Windrunner♒  </a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">All the books you mention have stories that take place on different planets, but are part of the same universe - The Cosmere. Elantris and the Emperor<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">All the books you mention have stories that take place on different planets, but are part of the same universe - The Cosmere. Elantris and the Emperor's Soul are set on the same planet though. <br /><br />Way of Kings, Elantris, Emperor's Soul are all part of the Cosmere and are thus connected. From what I remember, the planet way WOK takes place on (Roshar) is a very different place to the one Elantris &amp; TES takes place on (Sel)<br /><br />Why does the connection between WOK &amp; TES feel stronger to you ?<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://coppermind.net/wiki/Cosmere">http://coppermind.net/wiki/Cosmere</a><a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_370386'><a id="like_count_community_question_370386" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/370386?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">5 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F13578175-the-emperor-s-soul">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/15137105-squeak"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1371495256i/15137105._UY100_CR1,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/15137105-squeak">Squeak</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">No you do not need to read Elantris first. The Emperor's Soul can be read as a stand alone. You actually wouldn't even realize they were connected at <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">No you do not need to read Elantris first. The Emperor's Soul can be read as a stand alone. You actually wouldn't even realize they were connected at all but for the mention of one or two names.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

      });

<div id="review_1785626531" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1785626531" />
    <a title="Petrik" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59458347-petrik"><img alt="Petrik" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568016775p2/59458347.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1785626531?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Petrik" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Petrik" href="/user/show/59458347-petrik">Petrik</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59458347-petrik?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1785626531" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18319457612591576184"><i>(I read this in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded_The_Cosmere_Collection' title='Arcanum Unbounded The Cosmere Collection by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection</a>)</i><br/><br/><b>Absolutely incredible.</b> Apparently, 105 pages are sufficient for Sanderson to craft a fantastic story with a strong beginning, wonderful characterizations, memorable climax scene, and a satisfying conclusion.<i>The Emperor's Soul</i> has become <b>my favorite novella of all time</b>; it has qualities that surpassed a lot of other fantasy novels I’ve read.<br/><br/>I won’t go into any details on what the plot is, it’s only 100 pages long, try to jump into this sto</span>
  <span id="freeText18319457612591576184" style="display:none"><i>(I read this in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded_The_Cosmere_Collection" title="Arcanum Unbounded The Cosmere Collection by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection</a>)</i><br><br><b>Absolutely incredible.</b> Apparently, 105 pages are sufficient for Sanderson to craft a fantastic story with a strong beginning, wonderful characterizations, memorable climax scene, and a satisfying conclusion.<i>The Emperor's Soul</i> has become <b>my favorite novella of all time</b>; it has qualities that surpassed a lot of other fantasy novels I’ve read.<br><br>I won’t go into any details on what the plot is, it’s only 100 pages long, try to jump into this story without knowing anything about it as I did. The plot dances upon several themes such as the nature of humanity and what truly defines art. There was a lot of beautiful philosophical contemplation to be found here and the novella was utterly well-paced. <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> doesn’t waste any time getting into the plot; there’s no info dump, the magic system and world building were introduced gradually together with the plot and character development. Have I mentioned that the main character Wan ShaiLu (or Shai in short) is a lovable and intelligent heroine?<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“There was rarely an obvious branching point in a person's life. People changed slowly, over time. You didn't take on step, then find yourself in a completely new location. You first took a little step off a path to avoid some rocks. For a while, you walked alongside the path, but then you wandered out a little way to step on softer soil. Then you stopped paying attention as you drifted farther and farther away. Finally, you found yourself in the wrong city, wondering why the signs on the roadway hadn't led you better.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Everything about this book was stunning but the best part for me was definitely the Asian influences that can be found in the fantastic magic system and world-building. As an Asian myself, it’s always a joy to read a fantasy book that implements Asian culture with justice. Even though this is a short book, the magic systems—Forgery and Bloodsealing—were imaginative and intricately explained. as Sanderson’s usual strength. Sanderson has mentioned that <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> was created based on his experience in Taiwan; Forgery that relied on Soulstamp (Sanderson’s version of Chinese Seals), settings that reminded me of an older Asian palace, the clothes; the Asian influences were evident in every aspect of the novella.<br><br><b>Picture: <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> by <u><a href="https://www.deviantart.com/breath-art" rel="nofollow noopener">breath-art</a></u></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1561432595i/27721327._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lastly, although the setting of the world is in Sel, the same world where <i>Elantris</i>—Sanderson’s debut novel—took place in, you can read this novella without reading <i>Elantris</i>. There were only two or three terms from <i>Elantris</i> mentioned in the story and they served close to zero influence on the plot; you probably won’t even realize this book is related to it. Plus, in my opinion, this 100 pages novella significantly triumphed over the 600 pages in <i>Elantris</i>.<br><br>Impressive storytelling, unique premise, vivid and immersive prose made <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> a phenomenal novella that won the 2013 Hugo Award for Best Novella category justifiably. I totally recommend this book to anyone who’s looking for a short and superb reading experience. It doesn’t matter whether you’re a Cosmere fan or not, you don’t want to miss this reading this gem. <br><br><b><i><blockquote>“You can’t always write what you know—not exactly what you know. You can, however, write what you see.” </blockquote></i>–Brandon Sanderson </b><br><br>That’s precisely what he did, with brilliance.<br><br><i>Side note: The identity of The Imperial Fool can be found in this deleted prologue posted by Brandon Sanderson himself. Please read it only after you finished the book.</i><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://brandonsanderson.com/the-emperors-soul-deleted-prologue-imperial-fool/">http://brandonsanderson.com/the-emper...</a><br><br><b>You can order the book from: <u><a href="http://www.bookdepository.com/book/9781616960926/?a_aid=petrikleo" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Depository (Free shipping)</a></u></b><br><br><i>You can find <b><u><a href="http://novelnotions.net/2019/06/28/the-emperors-soul/" rel="nofollow noopener">this</a></u></b> and the rest of my reviews at <b><u><a href="http://novelnotions.net" rel="nofollow noopener">Novel Notions</a></u></b></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="18319457612591576184" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText7551918853786026467" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor's Soul by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor's Soul</a> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson" title="Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Brandon Sanderson</a><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1604313145ra/30323080.gif" width="480" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Complex, unique, and interesting.</i> Sanderson formed a very interesting and unique world which was surprisingly complex for its length with various related threads of ethical issues, political maneuvering, diverse character motivations, and engaging character interactions. The ending was very, very satisfying, and logical.<blockquote>
  <i>No matter how good you were, someone was better. Live by that knowledge, and you would never grow so confident that you became sloppy.</i>

<div id="review_2384744599" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2384744599" />
    <a title="Anne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1720620-anne"><img alt="Anne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415374035p2/1720620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2384744599?book_show_action=true">May 16, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne" href="/user/show/1720620-anne">Anne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=short-stories">short-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2384744599" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15500766287248103935"><b>What if you could create anything? </b><br/>Or more specifically, what if you could change the history of an object and essentially recreate what it believes it is?<br/><i>All you need is a little Titanium White...</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526479256ra/25550204.gif' width='375' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ok. Maybe not. <br/>Shai is a Forger who got pinched by the Imperial po-po while trying to steal some of their shit, and now, in exchange for her freedom, she's been tasked with recreating the <b>Emperor's Soul</b>!<br/><i>Which, in case you were wondering is why the book is titled, <b>The Emperor's Soul.</b></i><br/>Now, she's got to do</span>
  <span id="freeText15500766287248103935" style="display:none"><b>What if you could create anything? </b><br>Or more specifically, what if you could change the history of an object and essentially recreate what it believes it is?<br><i>All you need is a little Titanium White...</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526479256ra/25550204.gif" width="375" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok. Maybe not. <br>Shai is a Forger who got pinched by the Imperial po-po while trying to steal some of their shit, and now, in exchange for her freedom, she's been tasked with recreating the <b>Emperor's Soul</b>!<br><i>Which, in case you were wondering is why the book is titled, <b>The Emperor's Soul.</b></i><br>Now, she's got to do this in secret because the dude's been left a vegetable due to a failed assassination attempt.<br>Of course, creating (or recreating, in this case) a soul is next to impossible even if you had years to work on it, and Shai most certainly <i>does not</i> have years. She's got a few months before the Emperor's council needs to present him as hale and hearty to the other factions within the government who want to take over.<br><b>So what's a girl to do?</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526481021ra/25550510.gif" width="375" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, that's <i>one</i> option.<br>But Shai has other plans...<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526480058ra/25550288.gif" width="375" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was a really good short story, and if Sanderson's other fantasy stuff is anything like this, then I can't wait to read more!</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57236678-iryna-book-and-sword?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57236678-iryna-book-and-sword?shelf=brandon-sanderson">brandon-sanderson</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2076632949" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10194896875665827708">*3/28/2020<br/>Second read. Just as amazing. <br/>________________________________ <br/><br/><br/><b>"The Emperor's Soul"</b> deserves all of the stars. All of the praise.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>“There was rarely an obvious branching point in a person's life. People changed slowly, over time. You didn't take on step, then find yourself in a completely new location. Then you stopped paying attention as you drifted farther and farther away. ”</b>
</i><br/><br/>You know what this book's only flaw is? It's way too short.<br/>Oh, don't worry, the story is all perfectly wrapp</span>
  <span id="freeText10194896875665827708" style="display:none">*3/28/2020<br />Second read. Just as amazing. <br />________________________________ <br /><br /><br /><b>"The Emperor's Soul"</b> deserves all of the stars. All of the praise.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“There was rarely an obvious branching point in a person's life. People changed slowly, over time. You didn't take on step, then find yourself in a completely new location. Then you stopped paying attention as you drifted farther and farther away. ”</b>
</i><br /><br />You know what this book's only flaw is? It's way too short.<br />Oh, don't worry, the story is all perfectly wrapped up and beautiful. There just needs to be more of this because <b>"The Emperor's soul" is a masterpiece.</b> I could easily read 500 more pages of this.<br /><br />That said, this is the best thing I've read this year and it's only 175 pages. The novella is a Hugo Award Winner and I definitely see why.<br /><br />​175 pages to develop a <b>page turning story with deep background and great characters.</b><br />175 pages to create one of the <b>best female main character ever.</b><br />175 pages to have reader guessing the next <b>turn and twist.</b><br />175 pages apparently was all Brandon Sanderson needed to <b>blow my mind.</b><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“She took a deep breath and let herself become someone else. An imitation of herself who was calm, even in a situation like this.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Sanderson has an uncanny ability to write amazing female characters. I've noticed that since the very first pages <b>Vin (Mistborn) </b>was introduced, and once again from the very first pages of <b>Shai</b> in this book. First of all Shai wears glasses! Hello, I haven't ever read of a girl in a book, let alone fantasy book, who wears glasses! So, as a fellow glass wearer, I approve of this a 100 percent.<br /><br />Shai is both overly confident and the most humble. She is brilliant. Yes, some of her morals might be askew, but she has a big heart and a shining soul.<br />What I find absolutely refreshing from Sanderson's books is that he never focuses on his character's appearances. It doesn't matter what a person looks like - what matters is how they behave themselves, how they present themselves and what their skills and talents are. I feel that this is a very important message to deliver in a world where everyone and everything is judged by looks.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“People,” Shai said, rising to fetch another seal, “by nature attempt to exercise power over what is around them. We build walls to shelter us from the wind, roofs to stop the rain. We tame the elements, bend nature to our wills. It makes us feel as if we’re in control.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Since this is a short novella I don't want to write anything that might give something away. All I'm going to say is - do yourselves a favor - read it. If you are not into fantasy - read it. Who knows, this might be the book that will get you into it. And if you are Sanderson's fan, but haven't read this yet- you are missing out big time.<br /><br /><b>"The Emperor's Soul"</b> is going on my all-time-favorite-books shelf and it will stay there forever and ever.<br /><br />My <a href="http://bookandsword.net " rel="nofollow noopener">WEBSITE</a><br />My <a href="https://www.instagram.com/book_and_sword/" rel="nofollow noopener">INSTAGRAM</a><br />My <a href="https://bookandswordblog.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">WORDPRESS BLOG</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10194896875665827708" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1203044318" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1203044318" />
    <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl"><img alt="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603085284p2/8734459.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1203044318?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl">Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=library-has">library-has</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1203044318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18228608057895349966">This is a marvelous short fantasy novel - I absolutely loved it!! Very possibly my favorite of all of Sanderson's works that I've read.<br/><br/>Wan ShaiLu, a magical forger, is captured and put under sentence of death for her crimes. But Shai is given an opportunity to escape her sentence: she is charged with magically forging a new soul for the kingdom's assassinated emperor, whose body had been repaired but whose mind was destroyed by the attack. Shai is given only a hundred days to accomplish this nea</span>
  <span id="freeText18228608057895349966" style="display:none">This is a marvelous short fantasy novel - I absolutely loved it!! Very possibly my favorite of all of Sanderson's works that I've read.<br><br>Wan ShaiLu, a magical forger, is captured and put under sentence of death for her crimes. But Shai is given an opportunity to escape her sentence: she is charged with magically forging a new soul for the kingdom's assassinated emperor, whose body had been repaired but whose mind was destroyed by the attack. Shai is given only a hundred days to accomplish this near-impossible task. And there are those waiting to kill her if she makes a wrong step, or trying to subvert her task for their own selfish purposes.<br><br>It was all fantastic: the characters, the complex motivations, the layered storytelling, the intricate magical system built on Chinese-type stamps. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427694715i/14307716._SY540_.jpg" width="130" height="139" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are some fascinating touches that add depth to the story. One of my favorite bits is how Shai uses her Forging talents to turn her grim prison room into a lovely chamber, including a cracked glass window:<blockquote>Attempts to Forge the window to a better version of itself had repeatedly failed; each time, after five minutes or so, the window had reverted to its cracked, gap-sided self.<br><br>Then Shai had found a bit of colored glass rammed into one side of the frame. The window, she realized, had once been a stained glass piece. It had been broken [and] rather than repairing it as it had been meant to be, someone had put ordinary glass in the window and left it to crack. A stamp from Shai in the bottom right corner had restored the window, rewriting its history so that a caring master craftsman had discovered the fallen window and remade it. That seal had taken immediately. Even after all this time, the window had seen itself as something beautiful.<br><br>Or maybe she was just getting romantic again.</blockquote>I love what this book has to say about the nature of art, and souls, and how people affect each other.<blockquote>He found himself weeping.<br><br>Not for the future or for the emperor. These were the tears of a man who saw before himself a <i>masterpiece</i>. True art was more than beauty; it was more than technique. It was not just imitation.<br><br>It was boldness, it was contrast, it was subtlety. ... It was the greatest work of art he had ever witnessed.</blockquote>I'm also amazed at how much Brandon Sanderson packed into 167 pages. I would have enjoyed reading more, but really, this felt like the perfect length for this story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18228608057895349966" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1260073810" />
    <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes"><img alt="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598297811p2/1452829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes">Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=year-2016">year-2016</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1260073810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer289709817701153268"><b>My only complaint about this book is that it should have been longer!</b><br/><br/>Shai is a forger, meaning that she can rewrite an object's history, thus making it into a new object. Such magic is considered taboo within the Empire, that is until they find themselves enlisting Shai's help to try and forge the soul of their fallen Emperor, Ashravan. <br/><br/>I don't know why I loved this so much, I think I was just completely entranced by the magic system. It depends wholly on the plausibility of any given thing to b</span>
  <span id="freeText289709817701153268" style="display:none"><b>My only complaint about this book is that it should have been longer!</b><br /><br />Shai is a forger, meaning that she can rewrite an object's history, thus making it into a new object. Such magic is considered taboo within the Empire, that is until they find themselves enlisting Shai's help to try and forge the soul of their fallen Emperor, Ashravan. <br /><br />I don't know why I loved this so much, I think I was just completely entranced by the magic system. It depends wholly on the plausibility of any given thing to be another thing, it's a mystical power that's rooted in an object's <i>potential</i>, and that is so cool to me. <br /><br />Even though this book was only 175 pages, I was able to get such a clear sense of the characters. They were so genuinely written, like I could absolutely go out into the world and find similar people. When a character feels real, their motivations become important to me as a reader. I love the process of feeling an author breathe life into their words. <br /><br />I'll say that if you're reading this and hoping there will be throwbacks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68427.Elantris__Elantris___1_" title="Elantris (Elantris, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Elantris</a>, don't. This isn't necessarily a bad thing, but there isn't really much that ties this book to Teod or Arelon or Elantris or any of the countries/cities previously mentioned. The Jindoese people pop up briefly but that is mostly it. <br /><br />Anyhow, another wonderful installment from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson" title="Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Brandon Sanderson</a>!</span>

          </span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16131932-the-emperor-s-soul">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer840665888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11478895661775955594"><b>Audible Daily Deal Sale until 28Jan18 <a href='https://www.audible.com/pd/Sci-Fi-Fantasy/The-Emperors-Soul-Audiobook/B009XEKR3O' rel='nofollow noopener'>$1.99</a></b><br/><br/><b>Buddy read with fellow Sandersonitis afflicted friends <a>Athena</a> & <a>Alexa</a>, and newly wrangled in buddy reader <a>Katie</a></b><br/><br/><b>4.5 Soulful Stars</b><br/><br/>Just a reminder that Brandon Sanderson is probably my favorite fantasy writer I’ve read 9 full length books by him and 2 novellas, he consistently never disappoints so I might be a little biased, but deservedly so. His worlds, his imagination, his magic systems, his surprise twists always amaze me. The Emperors Soul was no diff</span>
  <span id="freeText11478895661775955594" style="display:none"><b>Audible Daily Deal Sale until 28Jan18 <a href="https://www.audible.com/pd/Sci-Fi-Fantasy/The-Emperors-Soul-Audiobook/B009XEKR3O" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.99</a></b><br /><br /><b>Buddy read with fellow Sandersonitis afflicted friends <a>Athena</a> &amp; <a>Alexa</a>, and newly wrangled in buddy reader <a>Katie</a></b><br /><br /><b>4.5 Soulful Stars</b><br /><br />Just a reminder that Brandon Sanderson is probably my favorite fantasy writer I’ve read 9 full length books by him and 2 novellas, he consistently never disappoints so I might be a little biased, but deservedly so. His worlds, his imagination, his magic systems, his surprise twists always amaze me. The Emperors Soul was no different, it is a complete story with another strong female character and I was totally drawn into the story immediately.<br /><br />Even though this is set in the Elantris world it stands on its own. You could read this without knowing anything about the Elantris story line and be okay and probably enjoy it just as much. Again Sanderson made up an entirely new magic system and showed it beautifully throughout the story. He made characters that were complex and interesting as well as sympathetic. Shai is another strong female character and I loved getting to know her in this.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> No matter how good you were, someone was better. Live by that knowledge, and you would never grow so confident that you became sloppy.</i>
</b><br /><br />Shai is a forger, she has been trained to use specialized images in stamps to rewrite the past and change things in the present. The Emperor has been damaged beyond repair and Shai is the only hope to create a new soul for him. It is the hardest task she has ever been given and if she fails her life will be forfeit, hell if she succeeds they will most likely kill her too. Shai must figure out how to finish her task and stay alive.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“We may feel in control, but we never truly are unless we understand people. Controlling our environment is no longer about blocking the wind, it’s about knowing why the serving lady was crying last night, or why a particular guard always loses at cards. Or why your employer hired you in the first place.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Again another great story from BS, I could hardly pull myself out of the story to even submit a status update.<br /><br /><b>If you have never read a Sanderson book and you are wondering ‘would I like this author?’ this is a great book to try and just get a taste of how wonderful the magic, worlds and characters he creates are.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11478895661775955594" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1634995324" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1634995324" />
    <a title="Haïfa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54721988-ha-fa"><img alt="Haïfa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592921740p2/54721988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1634995324?book_show_action=true">May 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Haïfa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Haïfa" href="/user/show/54721988-ha-fa">Haïfa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54721988-ha-fa?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54721988-ha-fa?shelf=owned">owned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1634995324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13859407368887865500"><i>I read this novella in the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded_The_Cosmere_Collection' title='Arcanum Unbounded The Cosmere Collection by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection</a> along with my fellow brigdemen (and bridgewomen?) : <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste' rel='nofollow noopener'>Celeste</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/59458347-petrik' rel='nofollow noopener'>Petrik</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/53385361-luna' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sarah</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mary</a></i><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>No matter how good you were, someone was better. Live by that knowledge, and you would never grow so confident that you became sloppy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This is a re-read of the Emperor's Soul and while it was just <i>good</i> the first time I read it, this time I found it to be an exceptional masterpiece!! I'm truly speechless and I never experienced this fee</span>
  <span id="freeText13859407368887865500" style="display:none"><i>I read this novella in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded_The_Cosmere_Collection" title="Arcanum Unbounded The Cosmere Collection by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection</a> along with my fellow brigdemen (and bridgewomen?) : <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste" rel="nofollow noopener">Celeste</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/59458347-petrik" rel="nofollow noopener">Petrik</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/53385361-luna" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">Mary</a></i><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>No matter how good you were, someone was better. Live by that knowledge, and you would never grow so confident that you became sloppy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />This is a re-read of the Emperor's Soul and while it was just <i>good</i> the first time I read it, this time I found it to be an exceptional masterpiece!! I'm truly speechless and I never experienced this feeling before! But this time I truly took my time, savored every word, paid attention to every detail and put the book down from time to time to ponder some retorts or deep thoughts. This was one of the most quotable books I've ever read ! With his simple, yet elegant writing, Brandon Sanderson delivered a remarkable reflection on the complexity of human nature, on the passions that stir; forge or define a person, on the passing of time and how it changes us, remodel us and stifle the fire and dreams of our youth. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>There was rarely an obvious branching point in a person’s life. People changed slowly, over time. You didn’t take one step, then find yourself in a completely new location.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />In a little over 100 pages, Sanderson created a new Empire, a new magic system, new complex and compelling characters, and managed to include a brilliant philosophical reflection and detailed explantations and links to the Cosmere. My only complaint about this book is that it is short ! Too short ! And I think my frustration at its length was what made me give it 4 stars the first time I read it. But if you can write 100 pages and include this amount of information, details, complexity, thoughts and feels, than you deserve all the stars, and all the praise that can be given !! <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I suspect,” Gaotona said, “that a life full of lying makes reality and falsehood intermix.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I don't want to say more about the magic or the characters lest I spoil the surprises of the novella but really if you're fan of Sanderson and his Cosmere, this is an absolute must! And if you love philosophical reflection in your Fantasy, or if you're fond of Fantasy with complex and original magic system, this book is for you!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13859407368887865500" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1003663218" />
    <a title="Markus" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26681101-markus"><img alt="Markus" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421952301p2/26681101.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1003663218?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Markus" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Markus" href="/user/show/26681101-markus">Markus</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17213238-the-emperor-s-soul">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26681101-markus?shelf=cosmere">cosmere</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26681101-markus?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26681101-markus?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1003663218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12435784858038074001">This little book is Brandon Sanderson's true masterpiece.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>She was nearly there with this project. The emperor’s soul spread out before her, with only some few corners still shadowed. She wanted to see it through; she longed to find out if she could make him live again.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Shai is a Forger, an artist who can copy and recreate almost anything through the use of forbidden magic. Sentenced to death for the theft of a sacred imperial relic, she grasps her final chance to live, and to perform the great</span>
  <span id="freeText12435784858038074001" style="display:none">This little book is Brandon Sanderson's true masterpiece.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>She was nearly there with this project. The emperor’s soul spread out before her, with only some few corners still shadowed. She wanted to see it through; she longed to find out if she could make him live again.</i>
</b><br /><br />Shai is a Forger, an artist who can copy and recreate almost anything through the use of forbidden magic. Sentenced to death for the theft of a sacred imperial relic, she grasps her final chance to live, and to perform the greatest feat of Forgery imaginable.<br /><br />Whil Shai is an interesting protagonist, the true star of the show is found in the character of Arbiter Gaotona, an old, powerful man in the upper echelons of imperial society. While his colleagues are merely grabbing for retained power, the soul of Gaotona, the oldest of them, is much deeper than that.<br /><br />I very much enjoyed the relations to artistry and the creative process throughout the book, even as part of a suspenseful story. There is even discussion of ethics and belonging in terms of art. And once more, Brandon Sanderson has proved himself adept at creating interesting mechanisms of the supernatural.<br /><br />Finally, it is also a story about memory. And about identity. About how the two are so irrevocably intertwined in a person’s mind and soul. This is true both for the protagonist and her subjects. And, perhaps, for all of us.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12435784858038074001" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13513417154915135927" style="display:none">[4.5/5 stars] Mini Review: As my second time through this novella by Sanderson (this time experienced via graphic audio for a professional review), I liked the reread just as much. The basic premise is rife with authentic Sanderson creativity and world-building – a magic system using detailed stamps to reforge items into something new. I love reading about any magic element that requires a lot of skill, so the craft descriptions throughout the story were my favorite sections. I also thought the main character had a lot of interesting dualities. There were a few moments where her decisions surprised me, and I love that. Overall, of all the shorts from Sanderson (I think I’ve read them all), this is a top 3 for me.   <span id="freeText3404700546608252898" style="display:none">I loved everything that I've read so far by Sanderson; The Stormlight Archive, Warbreaker, Elantris and Mistborn (Cosmere is a vast place with amazing stories). So I knew I won't be disappointed here as well. Which I was not indeed. But, WHY was this so short?   <i>There was rarely an obvious branching point in a person’s life. People changed slowly, over time. You didn’t take one step, then find yourself in a completely new location. You first took a little step off a path to avoid some rocks. For a while, you walked alongside the path, but then you wandered out a little way to step on softer soil. Then you stopped paying attention as you drifted farther and farther away. Finally, you found yourself in the wrong city, wondering why the signs on the roadway hadn’t led you better.</i>

<div id="review_1946693810" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1946693810" />
    <a title="Celeste" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7317186-celeste"><img alt="Celeste" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481055226p2/7317186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1946693810?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Celeste" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Celeste" href="/user/show/7317186-celeste">Celeste</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7317186-celeste?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7317186-celeste?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7317186-celeste?shelf=best-books-i-ve-ever-read">best-books-i-ve-ever-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1946693810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15915377492169937753">Original review can be found on <a href='http://booknest.eu' rel='nofollow noopener'>Booknest</a>.<br/><br/>I am an unapologetic Sandersonite. I’m completely in love with the Cosmere Brandon Sanderson has created, and so far I’ve adored every story he’s crafted that is part of that greater whole.<br/><br/> One of the things I love so much about his writing is the size of the books, and the knowledge that he’s a prolific writer, so I never have to wait too terribly long for more of the story. And yet, somehow, this tiny novella is now one of my favorite things he’s writte</span>
  <span id="freeText15915377492169937753" style="display:none">Original review can be found on <a href="http://booknest.eu" rel="nofollow noopener">Booknest</a>.<br /><br />I am an unapologetic Sandersonite. I’m completely in love with the Cosmere Brandon Sanderson has created, and so far I’ve adored every story he’s crafted that is part of that greater whole.<br /><br /> One of the things I love so much about his writing is the size of the books, and the knowledge that he’s a prolific writer, so I never have to wait too terribly long for more of the story. And yet, somehow, this tiny novella is now one of my favorite things he’s written, right after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7235533.The_Way_of_Kings__The_Stormlight_Archive___1_" title="The Way of Kings (The Stormlight Archive, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Way of Kings</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17332218.Words_of_Radiance__The_Stormlight_Archive___2_" title="Words of Radiance (The Stormlight Archive, #2) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Words of Radiance</a>. It was beautiful and profound and made me think deeply. I just wish there had been more of it. This is going to be less of a review than a “deep thoughts inspired by a story” session, so bear with me. <br /><br />Shai is a Forger, a woman who can “flawlessly copy and re-create any item by rewriting its history with skillful magic,” according to the synopsis. And she is the very best at what she does. The story follows Shai as she attempts an impossible task. It made me question everything I believe about what makes art worthy of praise and what defines a person or object.<br /><br />Is a skillful forgery any less lovely and awe-inspiring simply because it isn’t an “original”? It requires just as much talent and even more attention to detail, along with research and study that the original artist never had to consider. King Solomon claimed that “there is nothing new under the sun,” so what constitutes originality? Art has always been incredibly important in my life. Should I not sing or write or play guitar unless I have something entirely new to say? The most we can hope for as artists is to say something that’s already been said countless times but in some new way. Because nothing is ever said quite the same way twice. There can be no perfect forgeries, not really. When you pour yourself into something, when you give your art everything you are, your blood and sweat and tears and heart and soul, there will be some originality there, in spite of what critics may say. There has to be, because you are an original. There has never been and never will be a copy of <b>you</b>, and thus everything you create bears the unique imprint of your fingertips, your soul, your <i>self</i>. <br /><br /><blockquote>These were the tears of a man who saw before him a masterpiece. True art was more than beauty; it was more than technique. It was not just imitation. It was boldness, it was contrast, it was subtlety. In this book, [he] found a rare work to rival that of the greatest painters, sculptors, and poets of any era. It was the greatest work of art he had ever witnessed.</blockquote><br /><br />Without getting into the story itself (because it’s a tiny thing and everyone should read it. If you’ve never tried Brandon Sanderson before, here is a fantastic place to dip your toes in the waters of his writing.), Shai’s power comes from her understanding of the three different Realms: the Physical, the Cognitive, and the Spiritual. Everything exists in all three realms. In order to influence an object in the Physical Realm, you must understand how it views itself in the Cognitive Realm. Following this line of thinking, all things have some sort of self-awareness, whether animate or inanimate. This fascinated me. I’m a Christian, and as such I believe that God created us in three parts as He Himself is Triune. We are body, soul, and spirit, our own self-contained imitation of the Holy Trinity. Thus, in order to truly understand ourselves, we must understand all of our components. If I’m physically as in shape as an Olympic athlete but am depressed and suicidal, am I completely healthy? No! I have to have my mind and my body and my heart all working as one to be happy and healthy and at peace. Sanderson has taken that idea and applied it to everything in Shai’s world. Others in that world find this belief system pagan and disturbing, but their opinions don’t shake Shai’s views. She’s quite possibly my favorite character Sanderson has created so far. At the very least, she’s in my top five. She’s an artist who sticks to her beliefs and cannot be swayed, which I respect immensely.<br /><br />There were so many other deep questions that vied for my attention as I read. What makes us who were are? Are we just the sum of our experiences, or are we more? Is a person’s personality and soul quantifiable? How well do you know those around you? Do you pay attention only to what benefits you, or do you observe people for their own sake? Do you admire art for what it is, or simply because it’s popular at this moment? Sanderson crafted a beautiful addition to his Cosmere with Shai’s story. And, though this is set in the same world as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68427.Elantris__Elantris___1_" title="Elantris (Elantris, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Elantris</a> and not <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7235533.The_Way_of_Kings__The_Stormlight_Archive___1_" title="The Way of Kings (The Stormlight Archive, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Way of Kings</a>, it helped me understand Soulcasting much better, even if it’s not quite the same magic system. There’s a lot to love in this novella, whether you’re already a hardcore Sanderson fan or if you’ve never read a word he’s written. Give this a try, and let Shai’s story leave her stamp your soul.<br /><br />Read in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded_The_Cosmere_Collection" title="Arcanum Unbounded The Cosmere Collection by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded: The Cosmere Collection</a> as a huge buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/53385361-luna" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/59458347-petrik" rel="nofollow noopener">Petrik</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/54721988-ha-foun" rel="nofollow noopener">Haïfa</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">Mary</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">Tweebs</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15915377492169937753" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_466482577" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/466482577" />
    <a title="Eric Allen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6229358-eric-allen"><img alt="Eric Allen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560117879p2/6229358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/466482577?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eric Allen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eric Allen" href="/user/show/6229358-eric-allen">Eric Allen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer466482577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11689101435380321665">The Emperor's Soul<br/>By Brandon Sanderson<br/><br/>A Review by Eric Allen<br/><br/>Due to his work on The Wheel of Time, Brandon Sanderson has not had much time over the last few years for working on his own books. As such, he has elected to write several novellas as sequels to his already published works to tide his fans over until he is freed up from his obligations to the Wheel of Time, and can put his focus entirely back into his own works. The Emperor's Soul is one of these books. Though not actually a sequel, it</span>
  <span id="freeText11689101435380321665" style="display:none">The Emperor's Soul<br />By Brandon Sanderson<br /><br />A Review by Eric Allen<br /><br />Due to his work on The Wheel of Time, Brandon Sanderson has not had much time over the last few years for working on his own books. As such, he has elected to write several novellas as sequels to his already published works to tide his fans over until he is freed up from his obligations to the Wheel of Time, and can put his focus entirely back into his own works. The Emperor's Soul is one of these books. Though not actually a sequel, it takes place within the same world as Elantris, though in a distant land, and with none of the same characters.<br /><br />Shai is a forger, a person able to create exact copies of anything through magic and an understanding of its history and its pieces. Imprisoned for the theft of priceless artifacts, leaving fakes in their place, Shai awaits the day of her execution. When the Arbiters, those who rule in the Emperor's name, come to her with a proposition, she has little choice to accept. <br /><br />The Emperor has been attacked in an assassination attempt, and though his wounds have been healed, his mind is gone, empty, like a blank slate. Shai is given the task of making a forgery of the Emperor's soul to replace the one that was lost in the attack, and she must finish within one hundred days. Additionally, she must find some way to escape in that time, because it is doubtful that she will be allowed to keep her life with the knowledge that the Emperor himself is a creation of hers.<br /><br />As she delves deeper into her work, it begins to consume her. She puts her all into it, though her life is in danger, because she needs to find out if she is capable of such an awesome task, unable to leave without finding out if her forgery will work or not, not even to save her own life.<br /><br />The Good? This book is short and sweet. It doesn't waste any time getting into the story and the characters. Sanderson has done a very good job of developing Shai as a person through her studies of the Emperor's life, and her philosophical discussions with those who hold her captive. The book is also has a very clever and well hidden message that I believe is a very important one. I'll allow you to find it on your own, if you are able to.<br /><br />The world feels real, the characters feel real, and they do things for very real motivations. The forgery magic system, and the religion of the Empire that teaches that it is an abomination are both very interesting, and allow for some very interesting discussions on morality and points of view. <br /><br />Shai's motives and desire to do what no one has ever done before are very well explained in her actions, and her diving deeply into the the task that has been placed before her makes for a very interesting and entertaining character.<br /><br />The Emperor's Soul is very well written. One of Sanderson's biggest criticisms is that his writing feels very stiff and sometimes lacking in emotion or passion. And though I do enjoy many of his books, I can see where that criticism's roots lie. But this book had none of that in it. It flowed along perfectly, and with the right emotional connections at the right places. Another of his greatest criticisms is that his stories are basically vehicles to show off his ingenuity with magic systems. While a great deal of this book deals with the magic system, and it's morality, the story itself is more about Shai and her motivations as a character this time around. And as such, I found this book to be a lot more entertaining than a lot of Sanderson's previous works.<br /><br />The Bad? This is actually a first. I don't have anything bad to say about this book. There isn't anything I can complain about. I might count its short length as a negative, except for the fact that the story was exactly the length it needed to be. Adding in more scenes would have been unnecessary and would have clogged the story up with things that the plot just didn't need.<br /><br />In conclusion, though this book was short, it was very good. It has an excellent message in it, and a great climax at the end. I very much enjoyed the discussion on morality that this book brings up, and found the dialog to be witty and clever. There is very little external action, but the book is no less entertaining for it. It's a great book for its size and I think anyone who likes the Fantasy Genre will highly enjoy this.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/6229358?shelf=read" rel="nofollow noopener"> Check out my other reviews.</a><br /><br />**It has come to my attention that Brandon Sanderson has won a Hugo Award with this book. It is well deserved, and I offer him my congratulations on such a prestigious award.**</span>
  <a data-text-id="11689101435380321665" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText9091754581384695723" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Each person was a puzzle.</i>
</b><br /><br />My first official read of 2018, read this first cause I know I'll love it and I wanted to start the year with something I'll love.<br /><br />This book is perfect, am still marveled by the fact that its even a novella, the way the plot unravels, and that ending, I did not see that coming, then again its Brandon Sanderson, I shouldn't be surprise, he is a genius.<br /><br /><br /><u> World building and Writing</u><br />Once again Brandon Sanderson wowed me, the world is so well depicted even though its a novella of just a few pages. I love the magic system in this book so much, its a but similar to soulcasting. But with this, runes or symbols are carved on stones then stamped on the object to be changed, or on someone to change personality, past, get abilities and the like. The writing is explicit and easy to understand, the book is written in third person multiple POV, but 80% is in Shai’s POV.<br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br /><b>Shai</b> is just the perfect female protagonist, she is smart, intelligent, confident, manipulative and also a forger. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>what we have before us is a master trickster, liar, and thief. Your best guards would eventually become clay in her hands.”<br />“Thank you,” Shai said.<br />“It was not a compliment.</i>
</b><br /><br />Despite her career of choice, she is also kind and a great artist that makes people wonder why she forgers instead of making her own art.<br /><br /><b>Gaotona</b> was a mystery for 80% of the book, I had no idea what side he is but am glad for what I found out.<br /><br />I also like Ashravan the emperor, Frava and Uru got exactly what they deserve.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10386180352608734481">Exquisitely lovely!!! I did not expect anything else!!!<br/><br/><b>*** 5 ***</b><br/><br/>This story is "The Emperor's Soul " from the World of Elantris and is about a master craftsmen forger, Shai, who can meticulously copy and re-create any item by rewriting its history with skillful magic, knowledge and will. The concept is that an object can be "persuaded" do believe ti is different to the point that it changes itself and could even become something completely different. However, that something has to be believable t</span>
  <span id="freeText10386180352608734481" style="display:none">Exquisitely lovely!!! I did not expect anything else!!!<br /><br /><b>*** 5 ***</b><br /><br />This story is "The Emperor's Soul " from the World of Elantris and is about a master craftsmen forger, Shai, who can meticulously copy and re-create any item by rewriting its history with skillful magic, knowledge and will. The concept is that an object can be "persuaded" do believe ti is different to the point that it changes itself and could even become something completely different. However, that something has to be believable to begin with, only then would the forgery stick and persist. I loved the idea that the world depends on how we perceive it and what our vision and belief can do to the reality we live in, choosing to make it better or worse. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"...“People", Shai said, rising to fetch another seal, "by nature attempt to exercise power over what is around them. We build walls to shelter us from the wind, roofs to stop the rain. We tame the elements, bend nature to our wills. It make us feel as if we're in control. Except in doing so, we merely replace one influence with another. Instead of the wind affecting us, it is a wall. A man-made wall. The fingers of man's influence are all about, touching everything. Man-made rugs, man-made food. Every single thing in the city that we touch, see, feel, experience comes as the result of some person's influence.” ..." </i>
</b><br /><br />This story packed a whole lot of emotion and thought in a very short space. A delight to the more cognitive-oriented reader. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10386180352608734481" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_357525790" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/357525790" />
    <a title="Nimrod Daniel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5175502-nimrod-daniel"><img alt="Nimrod Daniel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1344358412p2/5175502.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/357525790?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nimrod Daniel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nimrod Daniel" href="/user/show/5175502-nimrod-daniel">Nimrod Daniel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5175502-nimrod-daniel?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer357525790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6643049662053009750">Rating this book would be difficult, especially because it's a short novel so I'll go through some points:<br/><br/>Characterization – the book is focused on two main characters, and that's probably what made it possible to portray them so well. The characterization in this book is superb, sanderson even managed to develop these two characters throughout the book in a very believable way, and considering the length of the book he did an excellent job.<br/>Just don't look for humor, as there's no funny characte</span>
  <span id="freeText6643049662053009750" style="display:none">Rating this book would be difficult, especially because it's a short novel so I'll go through some points:<br /><br />Characterization – the book is focused on two main characters, and that's probably what made it possible to portray them so well. The characterization in this book is superb, sanderson even managed to develop these two characters throughout the book in a very believable way, and considering the length of the book he did an excellent job.<br />Just don't look for humor, as there's no funny character here, unlike other books by Sanderson. There're a lot of witty dialogues though :)<br />Definitely 5 stars here.<br /><br />Magic system – This book has a unique and very imaginative magic system. For the matter of fact, throughout the first half of the book there're a lot of explanations of how forgery works and there're also some explanations about its mechanics in the second half. Forgery is relatively a complex magic system (it's more complicated than Allomancy or Feruchemy for instance), and it would have benefited being included in a longer novel, as Brandon could have developed it more than what could be done in 170 pages.<br />4.5 stars (It's a 5 stars magic system, and any other author would get the fully 5 stars here for being imaginative, but considering what Brandon could have done with this magic system in a longer book I reduced half a star).<br /><br /><br />Plot – it's a short novel and it includes a relatively complex magic system, so the plot that can be squeezed in a 170 pages is quite limited, though the storyline here is good. Most of the book occurs in one room so don't expect for too much action.<br />The story has a fully closed ending (unlike Legion), and it's a very good one.<br />4-4.25 stars here.<br /><br />The Verdict – This story is more about characterization than anything else, and it's very well written. It's so clear that it's a Sanderson book, I'd have easily figured it up if I didn't know who wrote this book.<br />All in all, it's a very good short novel. Highly recommended to any Sanderson fan.<br /><br />4.25/5</span>
  <a data-text-id="6643049662053009750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Valliya Rennell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58882300-valliya-rennell"><img alt="Valliya Rennell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596694907p2/58882300.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3401309482?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Valliya Rennell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Valliya Rennell" href="/user/show/58882300-valliya-rennell">Valliya Rennell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781473212640" href="/book/show/26546888-the-emperor-s-soul">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58882300-valliya-rennell?shelf=d-cosmere">d-cosmere</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58882300-valliya-rennell?shelf=d-fantasy">d-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58882300-valliya-rennell?shelf=c-stand-alone">c-stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58882300-valliya-rennell?shelf=x-reviewed-books">x-reviewed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58882300-valliya-rennell?shelf=d-crime">d-crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58882300-valliya-rennell?shelf=a-4-25-stars">a-4-25-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3401309482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13563373201202040255">4.25 stars<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"We may feel in control, but we never truly are unless we understand people. Controlling our environment is no longer about blocking the wind, it’s about knowing why the serving lady was crying last night, or why a particular guard always loses at cards. Or why your employer hired you in the first place."</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This is definitely my favorite Cosmere work so far. Unlike the others I have read, this one takes a step back and <b>focuses more on the magic system and characters... not plot at all</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13563373201202040255" style="display:none">4.25 stars<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"We may feel in control, but we never truly are unless we understand people. Controlling our environment is no longer about blocking the wind, it’s about knowing why the serving lady was crying last night, or why a particular guard always loses at cards. Or why your employer hired you in the first place."</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />This is definitely my favorite Cosmere work so far. Unlike the others I have read, this one takes a step back and <b>focuses more on the magic system and characters... not plot at all really.</b> Shai is a prisoner of the Rose Empire on Sel. She is also a Forger. <b>As a last effort to save her life, she takes up the politicians' offer to Forge the Emperor, who just suffered a debilitating brain injury, a new soul</b> to keep the Empire from falling into chaos. As forces work against her, will she succeed?<br /><br />One of the greatest praises I always hear about Sanderson is that his magic systems are fabulous. I finally understand this through Forgery. I love how it is shown and explained through the task, Shai's thought processes and Shai's conversations with Gaotona. Forgery in itself is actually really interesting too, in all honesty I prefer it to Allowmancy! I honestly can't wait for the <i>Elantris</i> sequels because I really hope they will showcase Forgery.<br /><br />There is really not much I can say without spoiling. There was a moment that kind of felt like it was meant to further the plot or just add tension it didn't need. Other than that, this was great :D<br /><br />-----------------------<br /><u>Books in Cosmere:</u><br /><i>Mistborn</i>: <b>Era 1</b><br />#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3389254251" rel="nofollow noopener">The Final Empire</a>: ★★★.5<br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3410251885" rel="nofollow noopener">The Well of Ascension</a>: ★★★★.25<br />#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3442078799" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hero of Ages</a>: ★★★★.5<br /><b>Era 2</b><br />#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3496930320" rel="nofollow noopener">The Alloy of Law</a>: ★★★<br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3508676308" rel="nofollow noopener">Shadows of Self</a>: ★★★.25<br /><br /><i>Novellas / Short-Stories</i>:<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3535966379" rel="nofollow noopener">Mistborn: Secret History</a>: ★★★★.25<br />The Emperor's Soul: ★★★★.25<br /><br /><i>Standalones</i>:<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3255448522" rel="nofollow noopener">Elantris</a>: ★★★.5<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3544252651" rel="nofollow noopener">Warbreaker</a>: ★★★.75<br /><br /><i>The Stormlight Archive</i>:<br />#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3447229371" rel="nofollow noopener">The Way of Kings</a>: ★★★★★<br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3562334239" rel="nofollow noopener">Words of Radiance</a>: ★★★★.75<br /><br /><i>White Sand</i>:<br />#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3475366302" rel="nofollow noopener">Volume One</a>: ★★<br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3481530514" rel="nofollow noopener">Volume Two</a>: ★★★<br />#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3490072180" rel="nofollow noopener">Volume Three</a>: ★★★.25</span>

    <a title="Jo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14323468-jo"><img alt="Jo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434090906p2/14323468.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
