      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo" href="/user/show/14323468-jo">Jo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=gr2016">gr2016</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=books-i-love">books-i-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1259618581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15400198280605157019"><p>What a brilliant imagination Brandon Sanderson has!!! This book was AMAZING!</p> <blockquote>
  <i>Wan ShaiLu, was more than a simple con artist. So much more. She could change the nature of reality itself.</i>
</blockquote> <p>Imagine a world where there are Forgers who can change/rewrite the nature of objects and even of a person by using a Soulstamp. </p> <p>Wan ShaiLu is such a forger, one of the best there is. And when she’s caught replacing a famous painting with her almost flawless forgery, instead of being executed she’s offered a d</p></span>
  <span id="freeText15400198280605157019" style="display:none"><p>What a brilliant imagination Brandon Sanderson has!!! This book was AMAZING!</p> <blockquote>
  <i>Wan ShaiLu, was more than a simple con artist. So much more. She could change the nature of reality itself.</i>
</blockquote> <p>Imagine a world where there are Forgers who can change/rewrite the nature of objects and even of a person by using a Soulstamp. </p> <p>Wan ShaiLu is such a forger, one of the best there is. And when she’s caught replacing a famous painting with her almost flawless forgery, instead of being executed she’s offered a deal - Forge a new soul for Emperor Ashravan within 100 days and she may live. The emperor has been left without consciousness after a recent assassin attack, and what his council is demanding from Shai is near impossible.</p> <blockquote>
  <i>A Forger wasn’t a simple scam artist or trickster. A Forger was an artist who painted with human perception.</i>
</blockquote> <p>I can’t even begin to explain how truly magnificent this book was, how amazing it was what Shai could do. For Shai to Forge a new soul for the Emperor, she had to spend many days and nights learning his past, his history, in order to get his soul right, because if it wasn’t a true replica of who he was before it wouldn’t take. And the more she learned about the emperor, about who he was, who he wanted to be, and who he was in the end, the more she was determined to get everything right, to make him live again. Even more determined than she was to escape.</p> <p>With every book I read by this author, I’m once again amazed at what a fantastic imagination he has. The worlds and magics he create are amazing, and this book was incredible. Brandon Sanderson is my favorite fantasy author, and this book is a must read for all.</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="15400198280605157019" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2449462444" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2449462444" />
    <a title="Coffee&amp;Quasars" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/62223917-coffee-quasars"><img alt="Coffee&amp;Quasars" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560940056p2/62223917.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2449462444?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Coffee&amp;Quasars" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Coffee&amp;Quasars" href="/user/show/62223917-coffee-quasars">Coffee&amp;Quasars</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2449462444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7447305778460965067">I buddy read this with Maggie!<br/><br/>I’ve heard good things about Brandon Sanderson for years and it’s been a while since I’ve read any good fantasy, so I decided to give this a try. Needless to say it hit the spot. Not immediately. It took about 6 or 7 pages.<br/><br/>The premise in a nutshell: Shai (incidentally one of my favourite protagonists in recent years) is a Forger, capable of rewriting the history of an object (provided the new history is plausible and shares some common branching off point from the o</span>
  <span id="freeText7447305778460965067" style="display:none">I buddy read this with Maggie!<br /><br />I’ve heard good things about Brandon Sanderson for years and it’s been a while since I’ve read any good fantasy, so I decided to give this a try. Needless to say it hit the spot. Not immediately. It took about 6 or 7 pages.<br /><br />The premise in a nutshell: Shai (incidentally one of my favourite protagonists in recent years) is a Forger, capable of rewriting the history of an object (provided the new history is plausible and shares some common branching off point from the original) or indeed, with a great deal of work, the history of her own being, remaking herself into someone with different skills, memories, thoughts and feelings. <br /><br />With an affinity for replacing priceless artefacts with her own Forgeries (which she considers an art in itself), she’s caught and given a choice: do the impossible by reforging the assassinated emperor’s mind in only 100 days, or be executed. <br /><br />In terms of the idea, the world and the magic, this could easily have been explored in a novel many times longer, but for this particular story, the length was perfect. Packed into a little over 100 pages, we have considerations of fate, choice, the nature of art vs plagiarism, authenticity, deceit as a way to tell the truth, telling the truth as a means of deceit, what it means to truly know a person, what it means to rule, what it means to be human and the difference between the kind of linear stories we tell about ourselves that approximate the truth, and the real thing. As Shai herself says:<br /><br />“A person was like a dense forest thicket, overgrown with a twisting mess of vines, weeds, shrubs, saplings, and flowers. No person was one single emotion; no person had only one desire. They had many, and usually those desires conflicted with one another like two rosebushes fighting for the same patch of ground.”<br /><br />I really appreciate Hard Magic systems over Soft, as I feel it makes for better storytelling when the rules are comprehensible by the reader and the hero isn’t allowed to pull just anything out of their ass at the last second. When someone goes deep into their craft, fictional or otherwise, I feel I’m able to sympathise with them, and/ or enter their world on a more intimate level. This book delivered on that front. There was another magic introduced called Blood sealing, considered separate from and far more nefarious than your typical Forgery. Though I can only speculate, there was one passage that for a brief moment made me wonder if they might both be different expressions of something deeper. <br /><br />In all, this was a 9.73 - Highly recommended. I’ll definitely be reading more Brandon Sanderson before the year’s out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7447305778460965067" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2974444089?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Manisha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Manisha" href="/user/show/29882975-manisha">Manisha</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17213238-the-emperor-s-soul">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">YA and Adult fantasy fans. </span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29882975-manisha?shelf=genre-fantasy">genre-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29882975-manisha?shelf=ultimate-faves">ultimate-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29882975-manisha?shelf=pages-101-500">pages-101-500</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2974444089" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6852535297502439890"><b>
  <i>“True art was more than beauty; it was more than technique. It was not just imitation.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>As someone who was wary of all the five-star ratings I saw given for this novella, I’m very surprised to know that I am now one of them. <br/><br/><br/>♥ <b>IMITATION OR ART</b><br/><br/>I absolutely <i>loved</i> this story about Shai, a talented Forger who is tasked with forging the soul of the emperor on threat of death. I loved it more than Elantris (clearly). <br/><br/>The entire concept of forgery, along with the lack of limitation as to what can b</span>
  <span id="freeText6852535297502439890" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“True art was more than beauty; it was more than technique. It was not just imitation.” </i>
</b><br /><br />As someone who was wary of all the five-star ratings I saw given for this novella, I’m very surprised to know that I am now one of them. <br /><br /><br />♥ <b>IMITATION OR ART</b><br /><br />I absolutely <i>loved</i> this story about Shai, a talented Forger who is tasked with forging the soul of the emperor on threat of death. I loved it more than Elantris (clearly). <br /><br />The entire concept of forgery, along with the lack of limitation as to what can be forged, the magic system which contributes and gives us rules as to how a forgery can occur and finally, the discussion of whether a forgery is a true work of art or not… Brandon Sanderson, you keep surprising me with your creativity and execution. <br /><br />This story was well rounded, well paced, well written and it needed nothing. That is a very rare quality in a story this short. <br /><br />I look forward to more.</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30279227-ts-chan?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer907238069" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13782146818903292941">Upgraded to 5-stars upon re-read. Initial read probably suffered from my post-Words of Radiance hangover. <br/><br/>Little wonder why this novella won the Hugo Award, so beautifully written and delivered, this story speaks to your soul - pun entirely intended. <br/><br/>Sanderson created yet again another imaginative magic system, Forgery, which is in short, imitation of the highest degree that requires a rewriting of history of the target. And what could be more complicated and masterful than that of the forgery o</span>
  <span id="freeText13782146818903292941" style="display:none">Upgraded to 5-stars upon re-read. Initial read probably suffered from my post-Words of Radiance hangover. <br /><br />Little wonder why this novella won the Hugo Award, so beautifully written and delivered, this story speaks to your soul - pun entirely intended. <br /><br />Sanderson created yet again another imaginative magic system, Forgery, which is in short, imitation of the highest degree that requires a rewriting of history of the target. And what could be more complicated and masterful than that of the forgery of a soul. <br /><br />He also gave us characters that are compelling (the relationship between Shai and Gaotana was simply wonderful) and injected emotion, tension and contemplation into a story which I can only describe as beautiful, all in under 200 pages. The magic system of Forgery was displayed to its fullest potential given the limited number of pages, but the essence of the story was not in the least compromised. <br /><br />One of my favourites from my favourite author. <br /><br />P/S: Do read the Postscript by the author :)</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣" href="/user/show/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat">Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=short-stories-novellas">short-stories-novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=less-than-200-pages">less-than-200-pages</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1428030093" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3172537210637973868"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul' title='The Emperor's Soul by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Emperor's Soul</a> is a nice, short book.<br/><br/>Shai is a Forger, a person who can copy and recreate anything with magical seals. While trying to steal an imperial relic, she was caught and sentenced to death. She was promised her freedom in exchange for recreating the emperor's soul (as he was left catatonic after an assassination attempt). <br/><br/>The book follows her imprisonment days as she creates the seal required for the emperor's soul.<br/><br/>I liked Shai's intelligence and intuition. She is fully aware that s</span>
  <span id="freeText3172537210637973868" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor's Soul by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor's Soul</a> is a nice, short book.<br /><br />Shai is a Forger, a person who can copy and recreate anything with magical seals. While trying to steal an imperial relic, she was caught and sentenced to death. She was promised her freedom in exchange for recreating the emperor's soul (as he was left catatonic after an assassination attempt). <br /><br />The book follows her imprisonment days as she creates the seal required for the emperor's soul.<br /><br />I liked Shai's intelligence and intuition. She is fully aware that she would not be left alive after her task is completed, so is constantly thinking of an escape plan.<br /><br />I also liked the lack of romance. Shai interacts mostly with 2 characters, Gaotona and Frava. Gaotona is a grandfatherly figure and an honest man, even if he is a politician. He genuinely cares for the emperor and wishes him back on the throne for more than selfish reasons.<br />Frava is also a politician and a cunning woman. She proposes that Shai make the emperor <i>inclined</i> to her suggestions in exchange for a position, all the while never meaning to hold her part of the bargain.<br /><br />Shai is torn between completing her task (as this would be her masterpiece) and her desire to save her own life. What does she do in the end? That's for you to find out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3172537210637973868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1838893980" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1838893980" />
    <a title="Scott  Hitchcock" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50894754-scott-hitchcock"><img alt="Scott  Hitchcock" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459187975p2/50894754.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1838893980?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Scott  Hitchcock" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Scott  Hitchcock" href="/user/show/50894754-scott-hitchcock">Scott  Hitchcock</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16131932-the-emperor-s-soul">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50894754-scott-hitchcock?shelf=epic-fantasy">epic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50894754-scott-hitchcock?shelf=sanderson">sanderson</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1838893980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer910000168856330418">Read as part of Arcanum Unbounded. <br/><br/>What amazes me in Sanderson's shorter works is how quickly and simply he creates a world. There's nothing superfluous or verbose about it yet it is engrossing and thought provoking. Definitely worth the read. <br/><br/>The postscript in Arcanum Unbounded about how the idea came about was very interesting after having the story just unfold. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('89rHE/Dl43GX4Yr3OcJrqc4bC69EFzCxtc6/IdxTg74w13Hr+25g+DuPXqlbGxlH5AeKqFXFqxJWwpKwiGYkOw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2DlL7Dd4fmYeAm6p21CYUl0a5wrQw0wgLrfb0HLj9AcbNP0UPPP977Jsuve5ieq8dwZmDcER14PNu/ZBJtZTgg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">About Brandon Sanderson</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1394044556p3/38550.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">Brandon Sanderson
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
154,109
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer18164712053267307414">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent' title='The Dark Talent' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded' title='Arcanum Unbounded' rel='nofollow noopener'>Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br/>Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul' title='The Emperor’s Soul' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Emperor’s S</a></i></span>
  <span id="freeText18164712053267307414" style="display:none">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent" title="The Dark Talent" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded" title="Arcanum Unbounded" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br />Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28698036.Mistborn__Secret_History" title="Mistborn: Secret History" rel="nofollow noopener">Mistborn: Secret History</a>,</i> and a brand-new Stormlight Archive novella, <i>Edgedancer</i>.<br /><br />Earlier this year he released <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704486.Calamity" title="Calamity" rel="nofollow noopener">Calamity</a>,</i> the finale of the #1 New York Times bestselling Reckoners trilogy that began with <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i>.<br /><br />Brandon Sanderson was born in 1975 in Lincoln, Nebraska. As a child Brandon enjoyed reading, but he lost interest in the types of titles often suggested to him, and by junior high he never cracked a book if he could help it. This changed when an eighth grade teacher gave him <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/176268.Dragonsbane" title="Dragonsbane" rel="nofollow noopener">Dragonsbane</a>
</i> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/10333.Barbara_Hambly" title="Barbara Hambly" rel="nofollow noopener">Barbara Hambly</a>.<br /><br />Brandon was working on his thirteenth novel when Moshe Feder at Tor Books bought the sixth he had written. Tor has published <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68427.Elantris" title="Elantris" rel="nofollow noopener">Elantris</a>,</i> the Mistborn trilogy and its followup <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10803121.The_Alloy_of_Law" title="The Alloy of Law" rel="nofollow noopener">The Alloy of Law</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1268479.Warbreaker" title="Warbreaker" rel="nofollow noopener">Warbreaker</a>,</i> and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7235533.The_Way_of_Kings" title="The Way of Kings" rel="nofollow noopener">The Way of Kings</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11543195.Words_of_Radiance" title="Words of Radiance" rel="nofollow noopener">Words of Radiance</a>,</i> the first two in the planned ten-volume series The Stormlight Archive. He was chosen to complete <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6252.Robert_Jordan" title="Robert Jordan" rel="nofollow noopener">Robert Jordan</a>’s Wheel of Time series; 2009’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.The_Gathering_Storm" title="The Gathering Storm" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gathering Storm</a>
</i> and 2010’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8253920.Towers_of_Midnight" title="Towers of Midnight" rel="nofollow noopener">Towers of Midnight</a>
</i> were followed by the final book in the series, <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.A_Memory_of_Light" title="A Memory of Light" rel="nofollow noopener">A Memory of Light</a>,</i> in January 2013. Four books in his middle-grade <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/623976.Alcatraz_vs__the_Evil_Librarians" title="Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians" rel="nofollow noopener">Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians</a>
</i> series have been released in new editions by Starscape, and his novella <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12796771.Infinity_Blade_Awakening" title="Infinity Blade Awakening" rel="nofollow noopener">Infinity Blade Awakening</a>
</i> was an ebook bestseller for Epic Games accompanying their acclaimed <i>Infinity Blade</i> iOS video game series. Two more novellas, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13452375.Legion" title="Legion" rel="nofollow noopener">Legion</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> were released by Subterranean Press and Tachyon Publications in 2012, and 2013 brought two young adult novels, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10137823.The_Rithmatist" title="The Rithmatist" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rithmatist</a>
</i> from Tor and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i> from Delacorte.<br /><br />The only author to make the short list for the David Gemmell Legend Award six times in four years, Brandon won that award in 2011 for <i>The Way of Kings</i>. <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> won the 2013 Hugo Award for Best Novella. He has appeared on the <i>New York Times</i> Best-Seller List multiple times, with five novels hitting the #1 spot.<br /><br />Currently living in Utah with his wife and children, Brandon teaches creative writing at Brigham Young University.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18164712053267307414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>

Yet each of these demigods was once an ordinary person until touched by the mysterious transforming power of the Shaod. Ten years ago, without warning, the magic failed. Elantrians became wizened, leper-like, powerless creatures, and Elantris itself dark, filthy, and crumbling.\n\nArelon\'s new capital, Kae, crouches in the shadow of Elantris. Princess Sarene of Teod arrives for a marriage of state with Crown Prince Raoden, hoping -- based on their correspondence -- to also find love. She finds instead that Raoden has died and she is considered his widow. Both Teod and Arelon are under threat as the last remaining holdouts against the imperial ambitions of the ruthless religious fanatics of Fjordell. So Sarene decides to use her new status to counter the machinations of Hrathen, a Fjordell high priest who has come to Kae to convert Arelon and claim it for his emperor and his god.\n\nBut neither Sarene nor Hrathen suspect the truth about Prince Raoden. Stricken by the same curse that ruined Elantris, Raoden was secretly exiled by his father to the dark city. His struggle to help the wretches trapped there begins a series of events that will bring hope to Arelon, and perhaps reveal the secret of Elantris itself.\n\nA rare epic fantasy that doesn\'t recycle the classics and that is a complete and satisfying story in one volume, Elantris is fleet and fun, full of surprises and characters to care about.       <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/19161502-the-emperor-s-soul">Quotes from The Emperor&#39;s Soul</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;There was rarely an obvious branching point in a person's life. People changed slowly, over time. You didn't take on step, then find yourself in a completely new location. You first took a little step off a path to avoid some rocks. For a while, you walked alongside the path, but then you wandered out a little way to step on softer soil. Then you stopped paying attention as you drifted farther and farther away. Finally, you found yourself in the wrong city, wondering why the signs on the roadway hadn't led you better.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/906751-there-was-rarely-an-obvious-branching-point-in-a-person-s">99 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Control yourself, she told herself forcibly. Become someone who can deal with this. She took a deep breath and let herself become someone else. An imitation of herself who was calm, even in a situation like this. It was a crude forgery, just a trick of the mind, but it worked.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/889046-control-yourself-she-told-herself-forcibly-become-someone-who-can">51 likes</a>
            </nobr>
